HIV (Human Immunodeficiency Virus) is a chronic, potentially life-threatening condition that attacks the body's immune system, making it difficult to fight off infections and diseases. If left untreated, HIV can progress to AIDS (Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome), which is characterized by a severe decline in the immune system.

If you suspect you have been exposed to HIV or are experiencing symptoms of HIV infection, it is important to seek immediate medical attention from a healthcare provider experienced in treating HIV/AIDS. 

Early diagnosis and treatment can significantly improve outcomes for individuals with HIV/AIDS.
